 The United Front of Transport Association is on strike against the new Motor Vehicle Act
 iske chalate dilli - ensiaar samet kai jagah logon ko dikkaton kaa saamana karnaa pad saktaa he
 If you too are going somewhere and if you have been facing problems due to the strike, then you can file a case for it and claim compensation
 is bare main lau professor vivek tyaagi kaa kahana he ki bharat main industrial dispute act ke tahat union ko hadtaal kaa kanoonee adhikaar diya gaya he
 Although this is not a fundamental right
 iskaa matlab yah hua ki transport sanghathanon ko hadtaal karne kaa moulik adhikaar nahin he
 This is just their legal right, that too with some restrictions
 lau professor vivek tyaagi kaa yah bhi kahana he ki hadtaal kii aad main koi sanghathan kisi duusare vyakti ke moulik adhikaron kaa hanan nahin kar saktaa he
 If a strike violates someone's fundamental rights, they can go directly to the High Court under Article 226 of the Constitution and Article 32 against the strike organization
 iske alaava hadtaal ke liye pehle se notice bhi dena hota he
 In addition, emergency facilities also cannot be obstructed
 is maamle main edwocket rohit shrivastav kaa kahana he ki hadtaal kii aad main koi sanghathan yaa vyakti manamaani yaa tod-phod yaa phir kisi kii awajahi baadhit nahin kar saktaa he
 If the strike organizations harass anyone or cause violence, both civil and criminal cases can be filed against them
 civil cese karne par peedit ko muaavja miltaa he, jabaki criminal cese karne par hadtaal karne vaale sanghathan or uske sadasyon ke khilaaf aapraadhik karrwai kii jaati he
 Advocate Srivastava says that a strike that harms law and order, sovereignty of India and any of these fundamental rights is illegal
 iskaa matlab yah he ki kisi sanghathan ko kanoon vyavastha yaa bharat kii samprabhutaa yaa kisi ke moulik adhikaron ke khilaaf jaakar hadtaal karne kii ijaajat nahin hoti he
 The police can also take action against illegal or violent strike
 iske alaava edwocket shobhit bharadwaj kaa kahana he ki kanoonon kaa paalan karte hue shantipurvak hadtaal kii ja sakati lekin agar hadtaal se aam logon ko baari dikkaton kaa saamana karnaa padataa he to aisi hadtaal ke khilaaf cese kiya ja saktaa he
 Many times a strike has to be made to get your point heard
 haalanki hadtaal kaa makasad kisi ko pareshaan karnaa nahin hona chahie
 Especially, this should not hurt the common people
 agar hadtaal ke dauraan chakkaa jam kiya jaataa he or logon ko dikkatein hoti hai, to yah gaiyrkanoonee mana ja saktaa he
